<script type="text/javascript">
    const consentAge = 18;
    const cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
    let pidValue = '';
    let hasPidCoppa = false;
    let isLoggedIn = false;

    for (let i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
        const cookie = cookies[i].trim();
        if (cookie.startsWith('pid=')) {
            pidValue = cookie.substring(4);
            isLoggedIn = pidValue.charAt(0).toLowerCase() === 'l';
        }
        if (cookie.startsWith('pid_coppa=')) {
            hasPidCoppa = true;
        }
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        const v = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + name + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
        return v ? v[2] : null;
    }

    function getAge() {
        const cookie = getCookie('pid_coppa');
        if (cookie) {
            const decodedCookie = atob(cookie);
            const splitCookie = decodedCookie.split('@');
            if (splitCookie.length > 1) {
                return splitCookie[1];
            }
        }
        return 99;
    }

    // Set up OneTrust object with Privacy Cross-Platform Consent Token
    if (isLoggedIn) {
        const privacyEncodedCookie = getCookie('privacyConsent');
        if (privacyEncodedCookie !== null) {
            try {
                const privacyCookie = decodeURIComponent(privacyEncodedCookie)
                // Parse the JSON string from the cookie value
                const { privacy_id, privacy_jwt } = JSON.parse(privacyCookie);
                // OneTrust object definition
                if (privacy_id && privacy_jwt) {
                    const OneTrust = {
                        dataSubjectParams: {
                            id: privacy_id,
                            isAnonymous: false,
                            token: privacy_jwt,
                        }
                    };
                    window.OneTrust = OneTrust;
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('PKW-Error parsing cookie JSON:', e);
            }
        }
    }
</script>

                            <h1 class="Article-headline">
                        2024 Paris Olympics medal count: Tracker for how many gold, silver, bronze medals USA, each country has won

<div id="Article-body" class="article article-main-body Article-body" itemprop="articleBody">
        
    
        
                
    <div class="Article-featuredImage">
                                <figure class=" img"><img class="Article-featuredImageImg is-lazy-image" alt="" data-lazy="https://sportshub.cbsistatic.com/i/r/2024/07/26/621439f2-109e-46f8-bdde-c9a4442fae23/thumbnail/770x433/307f5fcf1419beeb5c8cb3e352f87311/olympic-rings-eiffel-tower-g.jpg" src="" height="433" width="770"></figure>
        
                    <figcaption class="MediaShortcode-figcaption MediaShortcode-figcaption--indent">
                <span class="MediaShortcode-credit">Getty Images</span>
            </figcaption>
            </div>

    
    <div class="Article-bodyContent">
        
        
                            
                
        <p>The 2024 Paris Olympics continued Monday with a busy schedule including finals in 11 different sports. That included the team final in Men's Gymnastics, where the <span class="link"><a href="https://www.cbssports.com/olympics/news/2024-olympics-united-states-mens-gymnastics-wins-bronze-medal-ending-16-year-drought-in-return-to-glory/" target="_blank">United States won bronze</a></span>, its first medal since the 2008 Beijing Games. In the pool, U.S. Swimming followed up a strong Sunday with another solid showing, racking up <span class="link"><a href="https://www.cbssports.com/olympics/news/2024-paris-olympics-katie-grimes-emma-weyant-go-2-3-in-400-meter-im-to-highlight-dynamic-team-usa-swimming/" target="_blank">four medals across five events</a></span> and led by Katie Grimes and Emma Weyant going silver-bronze in the 400-meter individual medley.</p><p>That gives the United States a Paris Games-best 20 total medals, four ahead of host nation France. The Americans' three golds, however, rank just sixth so far. However, Team USA's men's and women's basketball are off to strong starts as Olympic gold favorites, and the women's soccer team -- also a strong contender for gold -- has also impressed. And USA Track &amp; Field performers are accustomed to produced results that often lead to multiple renditions of the "The Star-Spangled Banner."</p><p>The United States entered these games with the most Olympic medals ever won in the Summer Games. The U.S. also holds the record for most gold medals won in a single games with 83 captured in 1984, one of the country's host years which took place as the Soviet Union led a 12-nation boycott of the Los Angeles Games. Such lofty totals will likely not happen in 2024. In Paris, America is simply looking to build upon the success that it had three years ago at the Tokyo Games where the U.S. brought home 39 gold medals, 41 silvers and 33 bronze.</p>
        <div id="article-body-ad-0" class="native-story-ad">
        
        <div id="native_story_flex_top" class="ad-native-story-flex-top " data-ad="native-story-flex-top" data-ad-unit="native_story_flex_top">
    </div>

    </div>

    </td><td class="TableBase-bodyTd">0</td><td class="TableBase-bodyTd">0</td><td class="TableBase-bodyTd">1</td><td class="TableBase-bodyTd">1</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div></div></div>


        
            </div>
